name:Gâ€uâ€eâ€sâ€tâ€ â€Uâ€sâ€eâ€r
info:Superior Double Room
info:Stayed in October 2023
info:Family
info:7 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted October 4, 2023
msg:I came to Nanjing for three days and two nights during the National Day holiday and chose to stay here.
Nanjing Hexi CBD area, here is full of high-rise buildings and can be called Little Lujiazui. It takes no more than 10 minutes to walk to Yuantong Station of the subway. It is more convenient to take the subway to the attractions in the city. It takes less than half an hour to take a taxi to Niu Shou Mountain. The surrounding Huacai Tiandi is a large shopping mall. The next door Guojin Center is about to open, and it will be more lively in the future.
This hotel should be a business hotel with high buildings and many rooms. The rooms facing the main road have a wide view, and the Nanjing Eye Pedestrian Bridge can also be seen.
The room and bathroom are large in area, with both shower and bathtub, and double basin design.
The big bed is comfortable, and 2 pillows are provided. The quality of toothbrushes and other supplies is good, and disposable bathtub covers, gloves, alcohol cotton pads, hair ropes, etc. are also thoughtfully prepared.
The room is clean, and the hygiene and comfort are good.
The hotel automatically reaches the floor where you live by swiping the room card, which is highly secure. Different floors have different furniture design styles.
The buffet breakfast is on the 2nd floor, offering traditional Nanjing breakfast, more Chinese food, good taste, and a rich variety of Western pastries and fruits, including pig belly noodles and red stew noodles. The short holiday still hit the morning meal peak.
The lobby provides mineral water, ice drinks and thoughtful items.
It is a hotel worth staying in.
